<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спроектировать.html>спроекти́ровать</a> (30036)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проектировать.html>проекти́ровать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proektírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спроектировать.html>спроекти́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sproektírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проектировать.html>проекти́ровать</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to plan</li></ol>

***спрос.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спрос</a> (6017)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sprosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спрос</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spros</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спро́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спро́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спро́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> asking <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">the action of the verb to <a href = vnd.unilang:спрашивать.html>спра́шивать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́ть</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спро́са</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>sprósa</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">without asking (now idiomatic)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>demand (for something), market
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оживление.html>оживле́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спро́са</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oživlénije <b>sprósa</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">recovery <b>of (market) demand</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спрос</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предложение.html>предложе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spros</b> i predložénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">supply and demand</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">demand and offer</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спрос</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́треннем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рынок.html>ры́нке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spros</b> na vnútrennem rýnke</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>demand</b> within the domestic market</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спрос</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> что́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spros</b> na štó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">demand on something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>demand (for responsibility)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнок</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спрос.html>спрос</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ty ješčó rebjónok, kakój s tebjá <b>spros</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You're still a child, what can one ask of you?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́ть</a> (109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:просить.html>проси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sprosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрашивать.html>спра́шивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ask, to ask for, to inquire
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:девушка.html>Де́вушка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остановка.html>остано́вка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́буса</a>. The girl asked me where there was a bus stop near here.</dd></dl></li>
<li>to demand</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спрятать.html>спрячь</a> (21003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрятать.html>спрячь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sprjačʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">second-person singular imperative perfective of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спрятать.html>спря́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sprjátatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***спуск.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a> (5641)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spusk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спу́ска</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спу́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спу́сков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lowering, hauling down, launch <i>(the ship)</i>, lowering, descent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спу́ску</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne davátʹ spúsku</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>(idiom)</i> to give no quarter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>slope
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:крутой.html>круто́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krutój <b>spusk</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">steep <b>slope</b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отлогий.html>отло́гий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otlógij <b>spusk</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gentle/easy <b>slope</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sear, detent</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">polygraphy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> imposition</li>
<li>drainage, discharge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>воды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:туалетный.html>туале́тного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бачок.html>бачка́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spusk</b> vodý iz tualétnovo bačká</i> ― <span class="e-translation">flushing of the toilet</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>release
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:затвор.html>затво́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spusk</b> zatvóra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shutter release (for cameras)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спускать.html>спуска́ть</a> (5413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пускать.html>пуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">puskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спускать.html>спуска́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spuskátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спустить.html>спусти́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let down, to lower, to sink <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to allow to descend</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опускать.html>опуска́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to launch, to lower (a boat)</li>
<li>to unchain, to unleash, to let loose</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ejaculate (sperm)</li></ol>

***спускаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спускаться.html>спуска́ться</a> (2184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спускать.html>спуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спускаться.html>спуска́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spuskátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуститься.html>спусти́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to descend, to go down</li>
<li>to go with the stream, to go down stream</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спускать.html>спуска́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spuskátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***спусковой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спусковой.html>спусково́й</a> (13143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spusk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спусковой.html>спусково́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spuskovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> release
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спусковой.html>спусково́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:механизм.html>механи́зм</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spuskovój</b> mexanízm</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>release</b> mechanism; trigger mechanism</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спусковой.html>спусково́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:крючок.html>крючо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spuskovój</b> krjučók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trigger</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>release</b> hook</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:спусковой.html>спусково́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рычаг.html>рыча́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spuskovój</b> ryčág</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a gun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>release</b> lever</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спуск.html>спуск</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">spusk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***спустить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спустить.html>спусти́ть</a> (3803)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пустить.html>пусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спустить.html>спусти́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spustítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спускать.html>спуска́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to let down, to lower, to sink <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to allow to descend</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опустить.html>опусти́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to launch, to lower (a boat)</li>
<li>to unchain, to unleash, to let loose</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ejaculate (sperm)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опустить.html>опусти́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спуститься.html>спусти́ться</a> (1672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спустить.html>спусти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spustítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***спутать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a> (7777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путать.html>пу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spútatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">спу́тывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mix up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тал</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:передавать.html>передава́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:распоряжение.html>распоряже́ние</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>spútal</b>, peredavája rasporjažénije.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He mixed up when passing the instruction (command).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to confuse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">экзамина́тор <a href = vnd.unilang:невольно.html>нево́льно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тал</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:студент.html>студе́нта</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ekzaminátor nevólʹno <b>spútal</b> studénta.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The examiner unwillingly confused the student.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tangle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нитка.html>ни́тки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná <b>spútala</b> vse nítki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She has tangled all the threads.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутать.html>спу́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spútatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***спутник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спутник.html>спу́тник</a> (2330)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:путник.html>пу́тник</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pútnik</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">traveller</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутник.html>спу́тник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spútnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутник.html>спу́тника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутник.html>спу́тники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спутник.html>спу́тников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a fellow traveler</li>
<li>satellite, moon <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a natural satelite of a planet</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>an artificial satellite of a planet or moon, sputnik</li></ol>
